translation of BSSN_RHS.nb from Zach Etienne's SENR project, from Mathematica into Lua symmath
found at https://math.wvu.edu/~zetienne/SENR/
coordinate basis: $x$, $y$, $z$
non-coordinate basis: $\hat{x}$, $\hat{y}$, $\hat{z}$
Using capital letters to denote non-coordinate basis... which I'm denoting individually with hats.
Rescaling transform to non-coordinate basis:
${{{e}^I}_i} = {\overset{I\downarrow i\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 1 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 1 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 1 \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{e}_I}^i} = {\overset{I\downarrow i\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 1 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 1 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 1 \end{matrix} \right] }}$
grid metric:
${{{\hat{\gamma}}_i}_j} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 1 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 1 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 1 \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{\hat{\gamma}}^i}^j} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 1 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 1 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 1 \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{{\hat{\Gamma}}^i}_j}_k} = {\overset{i\downarrow[{j\downarrow k\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \overset{j\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{j\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{j\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{{{\hat{\Gamma}}^i}_j}_k}_{,l}} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow[{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } \end{matrix} \right] }}$
state variables:
${{{h}_I}_J} = {\overset{I\downarrow J\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}} & {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{{h}_I}_J}_{,k}} = {\overset{I\downarrow[{J\downarrow k\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \overset{J\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{J\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{J\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{a}_I}_J} = {\overset{I\downarrow J\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {a_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}} & {a_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}} & {a_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}} \\ {a_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}} & {a_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}} & {a_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}} \\ {a_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}} & {a_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}} & {a_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{{\epsilon}_i}_j} = {{{{{{{h}_I}_J}} {{{{e}^I}_i}}}} {{{{e}^J}_j}}}} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}} & {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{{\bar{\gamma}}_i}_j} = {{{{\hat{\gamma}}_i}_j} + {{{\epsilon}_i}_j}}} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {1} + {{h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}} & {1} + {{h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}} & {1} + {{h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{{\bar{A}}_i}_j} = {{{{{{{a}_I}_J}} {{{{e}^I}_i}}}} {{{{e}^J}_j}}}} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {a_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}} & {a_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}} & {a_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}} \\ {a_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}} & {a_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}} & {a_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}} \\ {a_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}} & {a_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}} & {a_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{{\epsilon}_j}_k}_{,i}} = {\overset{j\downarrow[{k\downarrow i\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \overset{k\downarrow i\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{k\downarrow i\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{k\downarrow i\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{\hat{D}_i \bar{\gamma}_{jk}}} = {\overset{j\downarrow[{k\downarrow i\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \overset{k\downarrow i\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{k\downarrow i\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{k\downarrow i\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{{{\epsilon}_j}_k}_{,i}}_{,l}} = {\overset{j\downarrow k\rightarrow[{i\downarrow l\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \overset{i\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{y}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{y}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{y}}{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{z}}{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{i\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{z}}{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{i\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{i\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{y}}}_{,{{z}}{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{i\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{y} \hat{y}}}_{,{{y}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{y} \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} ${{\hat{D}_k \hat{D}_l \bar{\gamma}_{ij}}} = {\overset{j\downarrow k\rightarrow[{i\downarrow l\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \overset{i\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{x}}}_{,{{y}}{{y}}} & l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{x}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{z}}} \\ {h_{\hat{x} \hat{z}}}_{,{{x}}{{y}}} & {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}_{,{{y}}{{z}}} & {h_{\hat{z} \hat{z}}}_{,{{z}}{{z}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{\beta}^i} = {{{{ב}^I}} {{{{e}_I}^i}}}} = {\overset{i\downarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {ב^\hat{x}} \\ {ב^\hat{y}} \\ {ב^\hat{z}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{B}^i} = {{{{בּ}^I}} {{{{e}_I}^i}}}} = {\overset{i\downarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {בּ^\hat{x}} \\ {בּ^\hat{y}} \\ {בּ^\hat{z}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{\Lambda}^i} = {{{{\lambda}^I}} {{{{e}_I}^i}}}} = {\overset{i\downarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {\lambda^\hat{x}} \\ {\lambda^\hat{y}} \\ {\lambda^\hat{z}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
